***пресмыкаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пресмыкаться.html>пресмыка́ться</a> (21622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смыкать.html>смыка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пресмыкаться.html>пресмыка́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">presmykátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to creep, to crawl</li>
<li>to grovel <i>(before)</i>, to bow and scrape <i>(before)</i>, to fawn <i>(on)</i>, to lick the boots <i>(of)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раболе́пствовать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rabolépstvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подхалимничать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podxalimničatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***пресный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пресный.html>пре́сный</a> (12398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">прѣснъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prěsnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prěsnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пресный.html>пре́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">présnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пресне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пресне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sweet, fresh (water)</li>
<li>unleavened (bread)</li>
<li>tasteless (food)</li>
<li>stale, insipid, vapid</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пресный.html>пре́сная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вода́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">présnaja vodá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пресново́дный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">presnovódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пресса.html>пресс</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">press</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:престарелый.html>престаре́лый</a> (9023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">старе́(ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staré(tʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:престарелый.html>престаре́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prestarélyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>aged, advanced in years
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:престарелый.html>престаре́лых</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dom <b>prestarélyx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">retirement home; nursing home</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:престарелый.html>престаре́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:престарелый.html>престаре́ла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:престарелый.html>престаре́ло</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:престарелый.html>престаре́лы</a></span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their similarity to past-tense forms (compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стареть.html>старе́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">starél</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">he grew old</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, feminine <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стареть.html>старе́ла</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staréla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).</li></ul>

***преступно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преступный.html>престу́пно</a> (18887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преступный.html>престу́пно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prestúpno</span>)
</p>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***претендовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:претендовать.html>претендова́ть</a> (7050)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">praetendō</i>, + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претендовать.html>претендова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pretendovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to claim, to pretend, to aspire, to have pretensions</li></ol>

***претензия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:претензия.html>прете́нзия</a> (4964)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претензия.html>прете́нзия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pretɛ́nzija, preténzija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претензия.html>прете́нзии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претензия.html>прете́нзии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претензия.html>прете́нзий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>claim, pretension, title (demand for one's rights, or for someone/something one thinks they have the right to).</li>
<li>complaint, dissatisfaction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> formal complaint of a creditor/purchaser/customer expressing protest to a debtor/supplier/contractor on account of a contract violation.</li>
<li>pretense (an attempt to impress others by showing off some positive attributes).</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">реклама́ция</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">reklamácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жалоба.html>жа́лоба</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žáloba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амбиция.html>амби́ция</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ambícija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:претерпевать.html>претерпева́ть</a> (32382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпеть.html>претерпе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preterpétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпевать.html>претерпева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preterpevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпеть.html>претерпе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to suffer, to endure, to go <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпевать.html>претерпева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишение.html>лише́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>preterpevátʹ</b> lišénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to endure hardships/privations</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to undergo
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпевать.html>претерпева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изменение.html>измене́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>preterpevátʹ</b> izmenénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to undergo changes; change</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***претерпеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:претерпеть.html>претерпе́ть</a> (20291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>терпе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terpétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпеть.html>претерпе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preterpétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпевать.html>претерпева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to suffer, to endure, to go <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпеть.html>претерпе́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишение.html>лише́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>preterpétʹ</b> lišénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to endure hardships/privations</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to undergo
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпеть.html>претерпе́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изменение.html>измене́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>preterpétʹ</b> izmenénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to undergo changes; change</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>A rare past perfective participle <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпеть.html>прете́рпленный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pretérplennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or its dated equivalent <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претерпеть.html>прете́рпенный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pretérpennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is occasionally found.
</p>

***претить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:претить.html>прети́ть</a> (25261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">прѣтити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prětiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to threaten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pertiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:претить.html>прети́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pretítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to forbid, to ban</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hinder, to oppose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угождать.html>угожда́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перс.html>Пе́рсам</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:благоразумный.html>благоразу́мно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:претить.html>прети́ть</a></b> Македонянам?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ugoždája Persam, blagorazumno li býlo <b>pretítʹ</b> Makedonjanam?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">When pleasing the Persians, was it judicious to <b>oppose</b> the Macedonians?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sicken, to disgust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:претить.html>прети́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лесть.html>лесть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>pretít</b> lestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">flattery disgusts/sickens me; I <b>can't stand</b> flattery</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:претить.html>прети́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:побегушки.html>побегу́шках</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>pretílo</b> bytʹ u nejó na pobegúškax</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he <b>was sick</b> of being an errand boy for her</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преть.html>преть</a> (23136)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преть.html>пре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сопре́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">упре́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взопре́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опре́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rot
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сопре́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">soprétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stew
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">упре́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uprétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sweat
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взопре́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzoprétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(of skin)</i> to become intertriginous, to become wet and irritated in folds
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опре́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oprétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***преувеличение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преувеличение.html>преувеличе́ние</a> (12093)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преувеличить.html>преувели́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preuvelíčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преувеличение.html>преувеличе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preuveličénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преувеличение.html>преувеличе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преувеличение.html>преувеличе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преувеличение.html>преувеличе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>exaggeration</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преувеличить.html>преувели́чить</a> (10797)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увеличить.html>увели́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uvelíčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преувеличить.html>преувели́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preuvelíčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преувеличивать.html>преувели́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exaggerate, to overstate

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преуспевавший.html>преуспева́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preuspevávšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преуспевать.html>преуспева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preuspevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th colspan="2" bgcolor="EEF9FF" rowspan="2" style="vertical-align:center;"><a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>паде́ж</a></th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF" colspan="3" align="center"> ед. ч.</th>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преуспевать.html>преуспева́ть</a> (25642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преуспеть.html>преуспе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preuspétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преуспевать.html>преуспева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preuspevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преуспеть.html>преуспе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to succeed, to be successful, to prosper
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:преуспевать.html>преуспева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>preuspevátʹ</b> v žízni</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to get on in life</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to flourish, to thrive, to prosper</li></ol>
